msg:I often come to Hangzhou, but this is my first time staying in this hotel. The surrounding area is relatively quiet, and the interior design of the hotel is very spacious and high-end. Afternoon tea is served as soon as I arrive, and breakfast is also provided. The lady at the front desk is nice and the service is very enthusiastic. In addition, the buffet breakfast is also rich in variety and tastes good. It's a pity that I ate in a hurry and rushed to the meeting, so I didn't have much time to taste it. I'll come back next time.
